class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Senate">Senate</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Senate"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The city belongs to the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Senatorial_district_IV" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Senatorial district IV">Puerto Rico Senatorial district IV</a>, which is represented by two Senators. In 2016, Evelyn V\xc3\xa1zquez and Luis Daniel Mu\xc3\xb1iz were elected as District Senators.\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Symbols">Symbols</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Symbols"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The municipio has an official flag and coat of arms.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>57<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Flag">Flag</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Flag"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The flag consists of two horizontal stripes of equal size. The upper one is blue and the lower gold, which are the predominant colors in the shield, which is placed in the center of it. \n<sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris-58"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>58<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Coat_of_arms">Coat of arms</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Coat of arms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Based on a design by Alberto Vadi, the coat of arms was organized by Herman Reichard Esteves and Jos\xc3\xa9 J. Santa-Pinter under the direction of the Aguadilla municipal administration and was approved by the municipal assembly on June 29, 1972.<sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris-58"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>58<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Education">Education</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Education"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Public_schools">Public schools</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Public schools"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>In all of the island\'s municipalities, public education is overseen by the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Department_of_Education" title="Puerto Rico Department of Education">Puerto Rico Department of Education</a>. Aguadilla hosts the <a href="/wiki/Head_Start_(education)" class="mw-redirect" title="Head Start (education)">Head Start</a> Program for Aguadilla, <a href="/wiki/Aguada,_Puerto_Rico" title="Aguada, Puerto Rico">Aguada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Moca,_Puerto_Rico" title="Moca, Puerto Rico">Moca</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rinc%C3%B3n,_Puerto_Rico" title="Rinc\xc3\xb3n, Puerto Rico">Rinc\xc3\xb3n</a>, and <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n, Puerto Rico">San Sebasti\xc3\xa1n</a> and a number of private institutions.\n</p><p>As of 2018-2019 the following public schools were operational in Aguadilla:<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>59<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-A-Z_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A-Z-60"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>60<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<ol><li>Ana M. Javariz is a rural elementary school located in Urb. El Prado offering grades K-6 with about 215 students.</li>\n<li>Antonio Badillo Hern\xc3\xa1ndez is a rural, elementary school located in Monta\xc3\xb1a offering grades K\xe2\x80\x936 with about 327 students.</li>\n<li>Homero Rivera Sola is a rural elementary school located in Corrales barrio offering grades K\xe2\x80\x936 with about 153 students.</li>\n<li>Jos\xc3\xa9 de Diego is a rural elementary school located in Res. Jos\xc3\xa9 de Diego offering grades K\xe2\x80\x936 with about 242 students.</li>\n<li>Luis Mu\xc3\xb1oz Rivera is a rural elementary school located in Camaseyes barrio offering grades K\xe2\x80\x936 with about 206 students.</li>\n<li>Antonio Badillo Hernandez is a rural intermediate school located in Monta\xc3\xb1a barrio offering grades 7\xe2\x80\x939 with about 336 students.</li>\n<li>Ester Feliciano Mendoza is a rural intermediate school offering grades 6\xe2\x80\x938 with about 416 students.</li>\n<li>Benito Cerezo V\xc3\xa1zquez is a rural high school located in Borinquen barrio offering grades 10\xe2\x80\x9312 with about 435 students.</li>\n<li>Juan Su\xc3\xa1rez Pelegrina is a rural high school located in Monta\xc3\xb1a barrio offering grades 10\xe2\x80\x9312 with about 715 students.</li>\n<li>Salvador Fuentes is a rural high school located in Ramey base offering grades 10\xe2\x80\x9312 with about 288 students.</li>\n<li>Centro de Adiestramiento y Bellas Artes (CABA) is a school that specializes in the arts located in Ramey base. In 2016, it served about 500 students.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>61<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>Su Conchita Igartua de Su\xc3\xa1rez is a rural elementary school offering grades PreK\xe2\x80\x938, with about 768 students.</li></ol>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Higher_education">Higher education</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Higher education"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Aguadilla hosts the following universities:\n</p>\n<ul><li>Puerto Rico Aviation Maintenance Institute</li>\n<li>Aeronautical and Aerospace Institute of Puerto Rico (AAIPR)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Puerto_Rico_at_Aguadilla" title="University of Puerto Rico at Aguadilla">University of Puerto Rico at Aguadilla</a><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>62<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Ana_G._M%C3%A9ndez_University#Metropolitan_University" title="Ana G. M\xc3\xa9ndez University">Metropolitan University</a>, Aguadilla Campus<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>63<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Interamerican_University_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Interamerican University of Puerto Rico">Interamerican University of Puerto Rico</a>, Aguadilla Campus<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>64<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>Automeca Technical College<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>65<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>Puerto Rico Criminal Justice College, Aguadilla Campus (Puerto Rico Police Academy) Ramey Job Corps<sup id="cite_ref-Ramey.jobcorps.gov_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ramey.jobcorps.gov-10"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> also serves those who want to attain a higher education.</li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Aguadilla_Library_System">Aguadilla Library System</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Aguadilla Library System"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>There is a digital library in San Antonio Village and another in <a href="/wiki/Aguadilla_barrio-pueblo" title="Aguadilla barrio-pueblo">downtown Aguadilla</a> (Aguadilla barrio-pueblo).\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Health">Health</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Health"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>There are two major medical facilities in Aguadilla.\n</p>\n<ul><li>Hospital Buen Samaritano (Good Samaritan Hospital)<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>66<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>Aguadilla Medical Services<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>67<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li>\n<li>Sala de Urgencias San Francisco (road#2)</li>\n<li>Metro Pavia Clinic Aguadilla<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>68<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Transportation">Transportation</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Transportation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Aguadilla_airport.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Aguadilla_airport.jpg/170px-Aguadilla_airport.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="128" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Aguadilla_airport.jpg/255px-Aguadilla_airport.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Aguadilla_airport.jpg/340px-Aguadilla_airport.jpg 2x" data-file-width="432" data-file-height="324" /></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Hern%C3%A1ndez_International_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Rafael Hern\xc3\xa1ndez International Airport">Rafael Hern\xc3\xa1ndez International Airport</a> \xe2\x80\x93 View of the Passenger Terminal</figcaption></figure>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Air">Air</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Air"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Hern%C3%A1ndez_Airport" title="Rafael Hern\xc3\xa1ndez Airport">Rafael Hern\xc3\xa1ndez Airport</a> is located in the city of Aguadilla. In recent years, it has seen a resurgence as an international airport in the island, with several airlines planning flights to the <a href="/wiki/Contiguous_United_States" title="Contiguous United States">US</a> from Aguadilla.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2022)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Roads">Roads</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Roads"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Interstate <a href="/wiki/Interstate_Highways_in_Puerto_Rico" class="mw-redirect" title="Interstate Highways in Puerto Rico">PR-2</a> (Rafael Hen\xc3\xa1ndez Highway). Plans are underway for a new expressway, an expansion to existing <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Highway_22" title="Puerto Rico Highway 22">Puerto Rico Highway 22</a> (Jos\xc3\xa9 de Diego Expressway) from <a href="/wiki/Hatillo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Hatillo, Puerto Rico">Hatillo</a> and it will probably end at <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Highway_111" title="Puerto Rico Highway 111">Puerto Rico Highway 111</a>.\nThere are 13 bridges in Aguadilla.<sup id="cite_ref-bridge_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bridge-69"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>69<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Notable_people_from_Aguadilla">Notable people from Aguadilla</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Aguadilla,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Notable people from Aguadilla"><span>edit</span></a><span
